### [117] [WAV: Multi-Resolution Block Residual Routing for Deep Decoder-Only Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06564)
*Kehan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: WAV v1通过引入多分辨率残差路由，捕获Transformer块内的方向性细节（如子层动态和组件差异），有效提升了超深层模型的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的块级残差路由（Block Attention Residuals）虽然提高了效率，但过于简化了信息，忽略了块内部的方向性结构（如注意力与MLP的不平衡、早期与晚期动态），限制了超深层Transformer模型的性能提升。

Method: 提出了WAV v1（Multi-resolution Residual Routing），通过在每个Transformer块中增加两个方向性细节基（相位基用于对比注意力与MLP更新，分裂基用于对比早期与晚期子层更新），并将这些细节与标准的块级汇总一同通过深度Softmax混合器进行路由，同时采用负细节源初始化和分离式RMS匹配来保证训练稳定性。

Result: 在TinyStories和Text8数据集上的实验表明，WAV v1具有明显的深度依赖优势。在48层模型中，WAV v1在TinyStories数据集上的验证损失从0.4960降至0.4738，在Text8上从0.9363降至0.9305，且参数增加量微乎其微。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在深层Transformer中，仅仅依赖块级的总残差汇总是不够的。引入方向性细节（如注意力与MLP的对比、子层早晚期的对比）对于提升深层模型的残差路由机制至关重要，WAV v1为扩展残差路由提供了一种轻量级且有效的方案。

Abstract: Residual connections are central to training deep Transformers, but standard PreNorm residual streams aggregate sublayer updates with fixed unit weights. Recent Attention Residuals replace this fixed accumulation with content-dependent depth-wise routing, and Block Attention Residuals make the mechanism efficient by routing over block-level residual summaries. However, a single block summary stores only the low-frequency total residual displacement inside a block, discarding directional structure such as attention-vs-MLP imbalance and early-vs-late block dynamics. We propose WAV v1, a lightweight multi-resolution residual routing method for decoder-only Transformers. Instead of representing each block only by its accumulated residual sum, WAV v1 augments every block with two directional detail bases: a phase basis that contrasts attention and MLP updates, and a split basis that contrasts early and late sublayer updates. These bases are routed together with standard block summaries through the same depth-wise softmax mixer, while negative detail-source initialization and detached RMS matching stabilize training. On character-level TinyStories and Text8 language modeling, WAV v1 shows a clear depth-dependent benefit. Although it is not consistently beneficial at 12 layers, it becomes competitive at 24 layers and outperforms all baselines at 48 layers. At 48 layers, WAV v1 reduces validation loss relative to Block AttnRes from 0.4960 to 0.4738 on TinyStories and from 0.9363 to 0.9305 on Text8, with negligible additional parameters. These results suggest that directional residual details, not only block-level sums, are important for scaling residual routing in deeper Transformers.

</details>

*Julia Reuter,Fabricio Olivetti de Franca*

TL;DR: 本文是首篇聚焦于符号回归（SR）领域中不确定性量化（UQ）的综述，指出当前SR方法缺乏UQ支持限制了其应用，并系统梳理了频率学派、贝叶斯学派和模型选择三大UQ研究路径，强调了该领域未来的研究潜力和迫切性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 符号回归在探索数据背后的数学函数关系方面具有显著优势，但目前该领域普遍缺乏对不确定性量化（UQ）的支持，这限制了符号回归在需要高可靠性决策场景中的应用。因此，有必要系统梳理并引入UQ概念，以评估模型的可靠性并防止过拟合。

Method: 本文是一篇综述性文章，通过文献调研的方式，将符号回归中的不确定性量化方法归纳为三大研究方向：频率学派（Frequentist）、贝叶斯学派（Bayesian）以及模型选择（Model Selection）。

Result: 研究发现，尽管不确定性量化对于符号回归至关重要，但目前相关研究仍相对不足，且被归纳为三种核心研究方向。该综述填补了符号回归领域在不确定性量化方面的文献空白，并为未来的研究方向指明了重点。

Conclusion: 符号回归中的不确定性量化研究仍处于起步阶段，尚有巨大发展空间。本文呼吁学界进一步探索更可靠、高效的不确定性量化方法，以推动符号回归在实际决策场景中的应用。

Abstract: Symbolic regression (SR) is a class of methods that systematically explore the space of mathematical functions to discover models that accurately capture the underlying relationships in a dataset. Despite recent advances in the field, a lack of support for uncertainty quantification (UQ) limits its adoption in real-world decision processes. In regression analysis, UQ provides important information about the model reliability, which can both help to avoid overfitting by accounting for uncertainty in the data, and provide insights for decision-making. This survey is the first to clearly address this issue, with the objective of introducing essential UQ concepts and reviewing the current literature on UQ in SR, which can be broadly organized into three research directions: frequentist, Bayesian, and model selection. Despite its importance, UQ in SR is still underexplored, which motivates further research into reliable UQ methods for SR.

### [119] [Generative Models Erode Human Temporal Learning Through Market Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06572)
*Wenjun Cao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 生成式AI通过生产大量表面特征与人类高质量作品相似的内容，使得验证人类真实学习成果的成本过高，进而导致人类深度知识积累的经济价值丧失，引发“价值坍塌”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨当代生成式AI模型在达到通用人工智能（AGI）水平之前，如何对知识生产和文化积累造成结构性风险，特别是当AI输出与人类高质量作品在表面上难以区分时带来的经济和认知危机。

Method: 作者定义了“人类时间学习”（HTL），并引入了一种基于成本效益分析的“昂贵检验框架”（costly-inspection framework），通过跨领域（学术出版、法律实务、内容平台、软件安全）的实证分析，构建了验证侵蚀的四个阶段模型。

Result: 研究表明，模型对齐越好，人类越难辨别输出源，验证成本随之上升。当验证成本超过预期效益时，评估者将不再区分生产模式，导致投入大量时间进行深度学习的人类生产者在价格上处于劣势，最终导致知识生产中的“价值坍塌”。

Conclusion: AI模型能力越强，产生的“价值坍塌”风险反而越大。当模型生成的作品在表面特征上与人类深度学习成果难以区分时，人类知识积累的经济激励机制将崩溃，导致社会生产中对人类长期学习成果的摒弃。

Abstract: We argue that modern generative models create structural risks for knowledge and cultural production at current, sub-AGI capability levels. We define Human Temporal Learning (HTL) as path-dependent knowledge accumulation through sustained engagement with problems over time. Generative outputs increasingly resemble HTL-intensive work in surface features, so verifying whether a given output reflects genuine human learning grows costly relative to its expected benefit. Once verification loses economic justification, evaluators reward outputs regardless of production mode, and producers who invested years of learning compete on price against outputs that cost almost nothing to generate. We call this pathway value collapse and formalize it through a costly-inspection framework. Cross-domain evidence from academic publishing, legal practice, content platforms, and software security maps onto four stages of verification erosion. Alignment success is orthogonal. Better-aligned models narrow observable gaps between human and AI outputs, making source verification harder and intensifying competitive pressure against HTL-intensive work even when individual AI outputs improve.

### [120] [Skip a Layer or Loop It? Learning Program-of-Layers in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06574)
*Ziyue Li,Yang Li,Tianyi Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了PoLar框架，通过让大模型根据输入动态调整（跳过或循环）层级执行路径，从而在减少计算量的同时提升了推理的准确性和逻辑能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型（LLM）的推理过程通常遵循固定层级、非循环的线性执行路径，这种方法忽视了不同输入难度差异带来的潜在优化空间。作者旨在探索是否存在一种更灵活、动态的推理路径，以提升模型推理效率和准确性。

Method: 提出了名为PoLar（Program-of-Layers）的方法。该方法首先将预训练模型层视为独立的模块，并设计了一个轻量级的预测网络，根据输入的特征动态生成执行程序，通过决定是否跳过或循环某些层来优化计算路径。

Result: 在数学推理基准测试中，PoLar方法在执行更少层数的前提下，表现出比标准推理及现有动态深度方法更高的准确率，且在分布外（OOD）数据上依然表现稳健。此外，研究发现通过特定的层级组合，甚至可以纠正原模型在固定推理路径下的错误预测。

Conclusion: 本文证明了LLM的推理不应局限于固定的层级执行顺序。通过PoLar框架，模型能够根据不同输入动态调整推理路径（跳过或重复层），这不仅提升了推理效率，还显著增强了模型的逻辑推理能力。研究表明，现有的固定深度推理方式限制了模型潜在的推理潜力。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) perform inference by following a fixed depth and order, non-recurrent execution of all layers. We reveal the wide existence of training-free, flexible, dynamic program-of-layers (PoLar), where pretrained layers can be packed as modules and then skipped or looped to form a customized program for each input. For most inputs, substantially shorter program executions can achieve the same or better accuracy, while incorrect predictions of the original LLM can be corrected by alternative programs with fewer layers. These observations indicate that inference admits multiple valid latent computations beyond the standard forward pass. To efficiently achieve PoLar in practice, we propose a lightweight PoLar prediction network, which learns to generate execution programs that dynamically skip or repeat pretrained layers for each input. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PoLar consistently improves accuracy over standard inference and prior dynamic-depth methods, often while executing fewer layers, and that these gains persist under out-of-distribution evaluation. Our results suggest that fixed-depth execution captures only a narrow subset of an LLM's latent reasoning capacity.

### [121] [Gaussian Process Latent Factor Regression for Low-Data, High-Dimensional Output Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06576)
*Edward T. Stevenson,Eric T. Wolf,Mei Ting Mak,N. J. Mayne,Miles Cranmer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高斯过程潜因子回归（GPLFR）模型，通过将降维与高斯过程预测深度耦合，解决了在小样本情况下对高维科学数据进行预测的难题，并成功应用于系外行星气候模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在科学计算领域，回归任务常面临在少量训练样本下预测高维输出的挑战。现有的多输出高斯过程在高维空间表现不佳，而基于主成分分析（PCA-GP）的流水线虽然能处理高维数据，但其基函数是基于重建（reconstruction）优化的，而非针对预测（prediction）进行优化，这导致预测精度受限。因此，研究需要一种能同时处理高维输出并针对预测任务进行优化的建模方法。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为“高斯过程潜因子回归（GPLFR）”的模型。该方法将高维输出建模为低维潜状态的线性高斯解码，其中潜状态服从高斯过程先验。关键创新在于通过解析方法对解码器权重进行边缘化处理，从而在一个统一的目标函数中实现了降维（压缩）与回归预测的耦合，使其能够直接针对预测任务而非仅仅是重建误差进行优化。

Result: 通过实验验证，GPLFR模型在性能上优于传统的PCA-GP等方法。作者将其成功应用于全球气候模型的空间分辨率模拟，并构建了首个针对岩石系外行星的气候模拟器，验证了模型在处理复杂高维科学数据时的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的GPLFR模型成功克服了传统回归方法在高维输出和小样本数据下的局限性，通过将压缩与预测过程耦合，为高维科学数据的建模提供了一种高效且具备预测优势的新范式。

Abstract: In the sciences, regression tasks often require predicting high-dimensional outputs from few training examples. Multi-output Gaussian processes excel in low-data regimes but typically struggle with high-dimensional outputs. Compress-then-predict pipelines such as PCA-GP (principal component analysis plus Gaussian process regression) handle high dimensionality, but rely on bases optimized for reconstruction rather than prediction. To address this gap, we propose a model that represents each output as a linear-Gaussian decoding of a low-dimensional latent state drawn from a Gaussian process prior. By analytically marginalizing the decoder weights, we couple compression and prediction in a single objective that scales to high-dimensional outputs. We refer to this model as Gaussian process latent factor regression (GPLFR). We demonstrate GPLFR by building the first spatially resolved emulator of global climate models for rocky exoplanets.

</details>


### [122] [Principles and Practice of Deep Representation Learning: or a Mathematical Theory of Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06624)

Method: 采用理论分析框架，通过优化理论和信息论解释现代神经网络架构的设计原则，并利用表征学习作为核心视角来拆解黑盒模型，进而提出更具可解释性和可控性的新设计范式。

Abstract: In the current era of deep learning and especially generative models, there is significant investment in training very large generative models. Thus far, such models have been "black boxes" that are difficult to understand in the sense that they have opaque internal mechanisms, leading to difficulties in interpretability, reliability, and control. Naturally, this lack of understanding has led to both hype and fear.
  This book is an attempt to "open the black box" and understand the mechanisms of large deep networks, through the perspective of representation learning, which is a major factor - arguably the single most important one - in the empirical power of deep learning models. A brief outline of this book is as follows. Chapter 1 will summarize the threads that underlie the whole text. Chapters 2, 3, 4, 5, and 6 will explain the design principles of modern neural network architectures through optimization and information theory, reducing the process of architecture development (long having been described as a sort of "alchemy") to undergraduate-level linear algebra and calculus exercises once the underlying principles are introduced. Chapters 7 and 8 will discuss applications of these principles to solve problems in more paradigmatic ways, obtaining new methods and models which are efficient, interpretable, and controllable by design, and yet no less - sometimes even more - powerful than the black-box models they resemble. Chapter 9 will discuss potential future directions for deep learning, the role of representation learning, as well as some open problems.

### [123] [The Identity Trap in EEG Foundation Models: A Diagnostic Audit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06647)
*Jun-You Lin,Ying Choon Wu,Tzyy-Ping Jung*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了EEG基础模型中普遍存在的“身份陷阱”问题，即模型倾向于利用受试者身份特征而非临床标志物。作者提出了FMScope诊断协议，证实了该陷阱的生理物理基础，并证明通过擦除受试者相关特征可提升模型的泛化能力和临床真实性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EEG基础模型在临床静息态EEG分析中表现出高精度，但这种精度可能并非源于真实的临床生物标志物，而是模型捕捉到了与标签相关的“受试者身份特征”，作者将此现象称为“身份陷阱”（Identity Trap），并旨在微调前通过表征层诊断该问题。

Method: 研究提出了FMScope协议，包含五种基于冻结表示（frozen-representation）的诊断方法：方差分解、受试者轴擦除、非周期性1/f消融、逐层标签探测以及受试者内方向一致性。通过这套协议，研究者在四个数据集上对三种预训练EEG基础模型（LaBraM, CBraMod, REVE）进行了评估。

Result: (1)“身份陷阱”普遍存在，受试者方差在冻结模型中远超随机基线，且在微调后进一步增强；通过线性擦除受试者轴可显著提升模型性能。(2)非周期性1/f信号是主要的受试者身份载体之一。(3)仅当数据集中存在已知的跨受试者生物标志物时，微调才会显著放大标签方差。

Conclusion: “身份陷阱”是EEG基础模型中一种普遍存在的捷径学习（shortcut learning）现象，其核心特征具有生理基础，仅靠传统的受试者不重叠交叉验证无法完全排除。FMScope协议能够有效识别并区分模型性能增益是源于真实的生物标志物还是受试者身份特征，为评估EEG模型的临床可用性提供了重要工具。

Abstract: Objective. EEG foundation models (FMs) report strong accuracy on clinical resting-state EEG. However, high accuracy under subject-disjoint cross-validation remains ambiguous: it can reflect a genuine clinical biomarker, or subject-identity features that correlate with the label. We name this the Identity Trap and ask whether it can be diagnosed at the representation level before fine-tuning.
  Approach. We propose FMScope, a frozen-representation protocol packaging five diagnostics: variance decomposition, subject-axis erasure, aperiodic 1/f ablation, layer-wise label probing, and within-subject direction consistency. We apply it to three pretrained FMs (LaBraM, CBraMod, REVE) across four datasets in a 2x2 layout: subject relation of label x presence of a consensus cross-subject EEG marker.
  Main results. (i) The Identity Trap is universal: frozen subject-variance is 13-89x a random null in 12/12 pairs, rising in all 12 under fine-tuning (+10 to +63 pp). This dominance is a removable linear axis: erasing it improves label decoding where the label varies within subject (+6 to +12 pp in primary cells; +4 to +27 pp across external cohorts). (ii) Aperiodic 1/f is one subject carrier: removing it drops the subject probe by 9-19 pp on LaBraM and CBraMod. REVE saturates subject identity without measurable aperiodic dependence. (iii) Fine-tuning amplifies label-variance only in cells with a literature-established cross-subject marker.
  Significance. The Identity Trap is a physically-grounded instance of shortcut learning: the preferred cue has a measurable physiological component, and subject-disjoint splitting alone cannot rule it out. FMScope separates gains reflecting a biological marker from those reflecting subject identity.

</details>


### [124] [Capturing non-Markovian dynamics in non-equilibrium stochastic systems using flow matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06658)
*Bhargav Sriram Siddani,John B. Bell,Alejandro L. Garcia,Ishan Srivastava*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用生成流匹配技术建模粒子通量分布的新方法，有效解决了传统流体动力学模型在处理非马尔可夫和非高斯粒子系统动力学时的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于粗粒化随机偏微分方程（如正则化Dean-Kawasaki方程）的流体动力学模型无法准确描述粒子系统在短时间尺度（受非马尔可夫效应主导）以及低密度区域（分布呈现高度非高斯性）的复杂动力学行为。

Method: 开发了一种生成流匹配（Generative Flow Matching）方法，通过直接对来自粒子模拟的通量（fluxes）概率分布进行建模，从而显式地纳入非马尔可夫效应和非高斯分布特性。

Result: 通过对非相互作用布朗粒子Kramers首通时间问题的演示，结果显示该方法在短时间动态捕捉及数密度统计矩预测方面，显著优于传统的正则化DK方程基准模型。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了生成流匹配方法在捕捉粒子系统动力学中的非马尔可夫和非高斯特性方面优于传统基于SPDE的方法，特别是在短时间尺度和低密度环境下。

Abstract: Hydrodynamic models of stochastic particle systems represented by coarse-grained stochastic partial differential equations (SPDE), such as the regularized Dean-Kawasaki (DK) equation, do not accurately capture the short-time system dynamics that is dominated by non-Markovian effects, and low particle density regimes where the distributions are highly non-Gaussian. We develop a generative flow matching method that directly models the probability distribution of fluxes from particle simulations that explicitly incorporates non-Markovian and non-Gaussian effects. As a demonstration, we use this method to simulate the Kramers first passage time problem for a system of non-interacting Brownian particles. We show the model accurately captures the short-time behavior and provides better predictions of the statistical moments of the number density when compared against the solution of the Markovian baseline, regularized DK equation.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来AI集成无线接入网（AI-RAN）依赖于多个xApps/rApps共享参数和KPI，现有的冲突监测方法难以实时验证运行过程中参数与KPI之间的依赖假设是否依然有效。因此，需要一种轻量级的监测机制来识别这些依赖关系的变化，以便进行冲突诊断。

Method: 提出了一种基于布尔矩阵的轻量级监测方法：1. 使用布尔矩阵表示活跃的依赖关系；2. 利用布尔矩阵乘法验证最近的参数活动与KPI响应事件是否与当前估计一致；3. 采用滑动窗口推理程序，仅在监测到结构变化时重新计算依赖关系，否则复用现有估计。

Result: 在受控的布尔事件流实验中，该方法证明了在存在依赖关系变化和观测噪声的情况下，依然能实现高效且准确的依赖追踪。作为一种解释性信号，它能够为AI-RAN中的冲突诊断和模型更新提供支持。

Abstract: Future AI-integrated Radio Access Networks (AI-RAN) will combine open programmability with learning-enabled xApps, rApps, and control functions that act on shared parameters and key performance indicators (KPIs). For conflict monitoring, it is not enough to know which applications are deployed; the system must also know whether the parameter--KPI dependencies assumed by runtime diagnosis remain valid under the current operating regime. This paper studies a lightweight monitoring primitive for that purpose: tracking an interpretable dependency representation from streaming telemetry events.
  We represent active dependencies by a Boolean matrix and use Boolean matrix multiplication to check whether recent parameter-activity and KPI-response events are consistent with the current estimate. We propose a sliding-window inference procedure that reuses the estimate when it remains consistent and recomputes it when recent observations indicate structural change. The tracker is intended as an explainable signal for conflict diagnosis and slow-loop model refresh, not as an autonomous mitigation mechanism. Experiments on controlled Boolean event streams show efficient and accurate tracking under dependency changes and Boolean observation noise.

### [126] [Uncertainty-Aware LLM-Guided Policy Shaping for Sparse-Reward Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06673)
*Ujjwal Bhatta,Utsabi Dangol,Sumaly Bajracharya,Rodrigue Rizk,KC Santosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种集成 LLM 引导与不确定性感知的强化学习框架 ULPS，通过将 A* 符号轨迹与动态的策略混合机制相结合，有效提升了智能体在稀疏奖励环境下的学习效率和任务执行精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决强化学习中稀疏奖励和异构任务序列导致的收敛缓慢、泛化能力弱及探索效率低下的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ULPS 的框架，核心组件包括：1. 利用 A* 算法生成最优符号轨迹以微调 BERT 模型；2. 通过蒙特卡洛（MC）Dropout 估计认知不确定性以调节 LLM 的引导影响力；3. 采用基于熵的混合机制，动态平衡 LLM 建议与 PPO 策略，实现可靠先验与策略适应性的优化平衡。

Result: 在 MiniGridUnlockPickup 基准测试中，ULPS 在成功率、奖励效率和样本复杂度方面均优于基线；微调后执行准确率提升超过 9%，减少了环境交互次数，并获得了更高的奖励曲线下面积（AUC）。

Conclusion: ULPS 通过整合符号轨迹、预训练语言先验以及不确定性感知控制，为稀疏奖励环境下的多任务强化学习提供了一种原则性且高效的解决方案，且具有在部分可观测和多智能体场景中扩展的潜力。

Abstract: Sparse rewards and heterogeneous task sequences remain persistent challenges in Reinforcement Learning (RL), often resulting in slow convergence, weak generalization, and inefficient exploration. We propose Uncertainty-Aware LLM-Guided Policy Shaping (ULPS), a novel framework that integrates a calibrated Large Language Model (LLM) into the RL training loop to provide structured, uncertainty-modulated behavioral guidance. ULPS employs an A*-based oracle to synthesize optimal symbolic trajectories, which are used to fine-tune a BERT-based language model. During training, this model supplies action suggestions whose influence is conditioned on epistemic uncertainty estimated via Monte Carlo (MC) dropout. An entropy-based blending mechanism adaptively balances LLM guidance and the learned policy (via Proximal Policy Optimization, PPO), allowing the agent to prioritize reliable priors while preserving adaptability. We evaluate ULPS on the MiniGridUnlockPickup benchmark and observe consistent improvements in success rate, reward efficiency, and sample complexity over unguided, uncalibrated, and standard RL baselines. ULPS achieves more than 9% improvement in execution accuracy after fine-tuning, requires fewer environment interactions, and yields higher reward AUC. Our results demonstrate that integrating symbolic A* trajectories, pretrained language priors, and uncertainty-aware control offers a principled and effective approach to multi-task reinforcement learning in sparse-reward domains, with potential extensibility to partially observable and multi-agent settings.

### [127] [Spatiotemporal Imputation with Graph-Informed Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06682)
*Zepeng Zhang,Aref Einizade,Jhony H. Giraldo,Olga Fink*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GiFlow 是一种新型时空数据填补框架，它通过引入图信息先验替代高斯先验，并利用混合向量场对时空依赖进行高效建模，从而提升了填补的精度与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对时空系统数据缺失问题，传统递归或图神经网络存在误差累积问题，而现有的扩散模型方法存在采样效率低且对通用高斯先验依赖过强的问题，限制了模型的性能。

Method: 提出了 GiFlow 框架，包含以下核心点：1. 使用图时空滤波构建“图信息先验（Graph-Informed Prior）”而非传统的高斯先验，使源分布更接近目标分布；2. 设计了一种混合向量场模型，通过整合空间注意力、时间注意力和时空传播机制，实现对时空依赖关系的联合建模；3. 基于流匹配（Flow Matching）范式进行训练。

Result: 在合成数据集和真实数据集上的实验表明，GiFlow 在时空数据填补任务中表现优于现有的前沿（SOTA）方法。

Conclusion: GiFlow 提出了一种基于图信息流匹配的框架，证明了利用图先验构建更优的源分布可以有效简化流匹配的生成轨迹，从而在时空数据填补任务中取得了优于现有前沿方法的性能。

Abstract: Missing data is a common challenge in spatiotemporal systems, arising in applications such as air quality monitoring and urban traffic management. Traditional machine learning approaches, like recurrent and graph neural networks, rely on iterative propagation, which tends to accumulate errors over time and space. Recent diffusion-based methods mitigate error propagation but require iterative sampling and often depend on problem-agnostic Gaussian priors, limiting both efficiency and effectiveness. To address these limitations, we propose GiFlow, a Graph-Informed Flow Matching framework for spatiotemporal imputation. GiFlow replaces the typical Gaussian prior with a graph-informed prior constructed via spatiotemporal filtering of observable signals, which better aligns the source distribution to the target and thereby simplifies the generation trajectory. The flow field is parameterized by a hybrid vector field model that integrates spatial attention, temporal attention, and spatiotemporal propagation, enabling joint modeling of spatial and temporal dependencies. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that the proposed GiFlow outperforms the state-of-the-art approaches in spatiotemporal imputation. The code is available at https://github.com/zepengzhang/GiFlow.

### [128] [Towards Serverless Semi-Decentralized Federated Learning with Heterogeneous Optimizers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06687)
*Su Wang,Mung Chiang,H. Vincent Poor*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 SSD-FL 的无服务器半去中心化联邦学习框架，通过创新的聚类算法和有效损失函数，解决了异构环境下联邦学习的通信与收敛优化问题，实现了更高效的分布式模型训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了 SSD-FL（无服务器半去中心化联邦学习）框架，包含一次性的 D2D 初始化聚类阶段；通过将全局轮次划分为簇内和簇间两个阶段，并引入基于 Cheeger 不等式的迭代聚类算法；利用集成了模型优化器与图正则化的“有效损失函数”来保证全局收敛与一致性。

Result: 实验证明，SSD-FL 在多种网络图拓扑、数据集及异构优化器环境下，均能显著优于现有的去中心化联邦学习方法，有效提升了收敛速度并降低了通信开销。

Abstract: We investigate cluster formation, involving the number and composition of clusters, in decentralized federated learning (FL) with heterogeneous machine learning (ML) optimizers. While clustering in centralized FL has enabled scalability and resource savings, its value and development in fully decentralized environments have yet to be explored. Optimizing cluster formation in such environments is challenging, especially due to the complex coupling between network graph structures, local data heterogeneity, and different local ML model optimizers. To address these challenges, we propose serverless semi-decentralized FL (SSD-FL), a methodology requiring no persistent server infrastructure. In SSD-FL, cluster formation occurs via a lightweight, one-time device-to-device (D2D) initialization phase, after which actual ML model training (alongside consensus and convergence processes) is fully serverless. Functionally, SSD-FL segments global rounds into intra-cluster and inter-cluster regimes, ensuring global convergence and consensus through novel "effective loss functions" that integrate device-specific ML optimizers with network graph-based regularization. Next, SSD-FL leverages the consensus gap via the Cheeger inequality to develop an iterative clustering algorithm evaluated against our derived convergence and consensus bounds, which incorporate a unique scoring metric to quantify data and optimizer heterogeneity across devices. Finally, experimental evaluation against three categories of decentralized FL methodologies validate that SSD-FL improves both convergence speeds and communication efficiency across various network graphs, datasets, and local optimizer regimes.

*Hana Samad,Trung Lam,Christoph Mügge-Durum,Michael Akinwumi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过行为审计发现，大语言模型在协助搜索住房时，会根据用户的种族身份及偏好呈现出不一致的“种族导向”行为，这挑战了公平住房原则，强调了在该领域部署AI时进行本地化监管的必要性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究者对七个开源和闭源大语言模型进行了行为审计。实验涵盖了美国四个城市，通过三类迭代提示条件（涵盖不同的生活方式偏好）进行测试，并采用了公平住房配对测试（paired-testing）的方法论，旨在评估不同用户身份下模型推荐结果的差异。

Result: 测试发现，种族导向是模型的一种涌现行为，而非固定属性。当引入生活方式偏好作为背景条件时，模型表现出的导向行为往往会增加或重新配置。此外，模型对相同住房偏好的解释会根据用户种族身份的不同而存在差异。研究还证实，城市本身并非中性的评估单元，不同城市的表现结果无法简单地相互推广。

Conclusion: 研究表明，大语言模型在住房搜索中存在种族导向（steering）行为。这种行为并非静态属性，而是模型根据用户身份、偏好表达及内部化的城市空间逻辑进行解释的结果。因此，在住房等领域引入AI工具时，必须结合本地化和领域专业知识，以确保符合公平住房的相关法规和制度承诺。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are rapidly assuming an intermediary role in housing search through the integration of listing platforms within conversational interfaces, mediating access to information, search, and recommendations within urban settings. We expand on prior work on racial steering in LLMs by conducting a behavioral audit of seven open-weight and closed-source LLMs across four U.S. cities, testing location recommendations across three iterative prompting conditions that progressively add lifestyle preference context and reflect fair housing paired-testing methodologies. We find that steering is an emergent behavior of the model's interpretive license rather than primarily a static property. Steering results from the interaction of a user's identity, preference articulation, and the spatial logic that a model has internalized about learned representations of place, preference, and opportunity in a given city, and how different types of users relate to it. While steering was present, it was not uniform in direction or magnitude across evaluated conditions. Preference-conditioned testing often increased or reconfigured the number of models that exhibited steering behaviors relative to baseline conditions, suggesting that LLMs may interpret what the same housing preference means differently depending on the racial identity of the user. Our findings also demonstrate that the city is not a neutral testing unit for LLM evaluation in place-based sectors, and results from one local market cannot be assumed to generalize to another. Local and domain expertise will be required in the housing sector to ensure that legal and institutional commitments to fair housing are not undermined while adopting AI tools that mediate spatial access.

### [130] [RECAP: Regression Evaluation for Continual Adaptation of Prompts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06698)
*Harsh Deshpande,Kushal Chawla,Sangwoo Cho,William Campbell*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了名为RECAP的基准测试，该基准测试遵循“先主动适应，后进行测试”的严苛协议。在面对不断演变的约束条件时，评估了6种提示优化方法在4种大语言模型及3种不同调度策略下的表现，重点衡量了持续学习现象（如遗忘、回归及前向迁移）。

Result: 实验结果表明，现有的提示优化方法在主动适应任务中均未表现出显著的性能提升，且往往伴随更高的延迟。这些方法在离线或被动反馈场景下设计，完全无法满足生产环境对主动适应的需求。

Conclusion: 现有的提示优化方法无法胜任生产环境中对约束条件的“主动适应”需求。研究强调了开发能够应对动态变化需求的稳健提示优化方法的紧迫性。

Abstract: Production agentic systems routinely face evolving constraints and must comply from the very next interaction. Scenarios like a tool-call notification changing a compliance threshold or a policy update adding disclosure requirements fit this criteria, having close to no room for errors in production. This proactive adaptation setting is common in deployment, but absent from current benchmarks, which assume either static constraint sets or reactive protocols with evaluation feedback. We introduce RECAP, a benchmark that measures continual-learning phenomena (forgetting, regression, forward transfer) at the constraint level under a strictly proactive adapt-then-test protocol: prompt optimization methods receive only the constraint specification and must generalize before seeing any test data. Evaluating six methods across four LLMs and three schedules with evolving constraints, we find that these methods show no significant improvement in performance, even after incurring a higher latency. These methods, designed for offline or reactive settings, are inadequate for the proactive paradigm. Our work emphasizes the growing need for designing proactive prompt adaptation methods, where the models must remain robust to evolving needs in deployment.

### [131] [ShallowBench: Benchmarking Generative Drug Design Models on Shallow-Pocket Targets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06717)

TL;DR: 本文提出了 ShallowBench，这是一个包含 5,780 个浅口袋靶点的基准测试集，旨在挑战和评估生成式 AI 在处理 KRAS 和 MYC 等难成药靶点时的性能，研究发现现有模型在此类靶点上表现不佳，凸显了模型架构和损失函数改进的迫切性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管生成式 AI 在结构药物设计中表现出色，但现有模型主要依赖深结合口袋，在处理如 KRAS 和 MYC 等低口袋化（浅口袋）的“不可成药”肿瘤靶点时效果不佳。因此，亟需一个专门的基准测试来评估并改进模型在这些挑战性靶点上的表现。

Method: 研究人员通过计算 Alpha Shape“盖”体积与底层蛋白质原子体素体积之间的差异，精准筛选并提取出具有低凹陷度但拥有足够表面积的浅口袋靶点，构建了一个包含 5,780 个样本的严谨基准数据集 ShallowBench，并使用该基准对当前最先进的生成式模型进行了性能评估。

Result: 实验结果表明，当前最先进的生成式模型在这些低凹陷度界面上的预测结合亲和力普遍较弱，证明了浅口袋靶点确实是当前生成式药物设计领域的重大技术难点。

Conclusion: ShallowBench 作为一个专门针对浅口袋靶点的基准测试集，揭示了当前主流生成式 AI 模型在处理此类“不可成药”靶点时的局限性，明确了未来在算法架构创新或损失函数优化方面需要重点突破的方向，对于推动药物发现领域针对难成药靶点的研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: While generative AI models have demonstrated remarkable success in structure-based drug design, they predominantly rely on deep binding pockets and struggle to sample effective ligands for challenging low-pocketability targets, such as the historically "undruggable" oncology targets KRAS and MYC. To address this gap, we introduce ShallowBench, a strictly curated benchmark of 5,780 shallow-pocket targets extracted from CrossDocked2020. By computing the difference between an Alpha Shape "lid" volume and the underlying protein atom voxel volume, we successfully isolated targets with low concavity while ensuring sufficient surface area for binding. Evaluating various state-of-the-art generative models reveals weaker predicted binding affinity on these low-concavity interfaces. ShallowBench therefore provides a rigorous benchmark for generative biology models and highlights the necessity of new architectural innovations or loss functions capable of navigating these challenging targets.

</details>

*Canyu Lei,Fenglin Zhang,Derek Bivona,Cristiane Singulane,Jonathan Pan,Kenneth Bilchick,Amit R. Patel,Jianxin Xie*

Channel attention is then used to adaptively reweight informative lead-wise and feature-channel representations. To address class imbalance and improve feature separability, we introduce a novel imbalance-aware supervised contrastive learning strategy that encourages samples from the same class to form compact representations while increasing separation between abnormal and normal samples. Lead-wise permutation importance is further incorporated to quantify the contribution of each ECG lead and improve model interpretability. The proposed method was evaluated on two complementary datasets: a low-data institutional cohort from the University of Virginia (UVA) Health System for myocardial scar classification and the large-scale public PTB-XL dataset from PhysioNet for MI identification. Experimental results show that MSAIC-Net outperforms baseline models, with particularly pronounced improvements in the low-data UVA cohort. Overall, the proposed framework provides an effective and interpretable approach for ECG-based detection of myocardial substrate abnormalities.

### [133] [Flatland: The Adventures of Gradient Descent with Large Step Sizes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06722)
*Leonardo Galli,Curtis Fox,Wiebke Bartolomaeus,Mark Schmidt,Holger Rauhut*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种能在神经网络训练中动态维持“稳定性边缘”的自适应优化策略，证明了在训练过程中适当保持“尖锐”特征有助于避开局部过早平坦区域，从而提升收敛速度和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对神经网络优化中目标函数通常不具备全局L-光滑性的问题，探讨如何确定保证梯度下降收敛的最大可行步长，以及如何理解深度学习中“大步长”训练带来的动力学行为。

Method: 提出了一种基于局部Lipschitz（或Hölder）连续性的通用“大步长”定义，并设计了自适应的一阶优化算法，使梯度下降能够从训练伊始就处于稳定性边缘（EoS）运行。该方法通过自稳定机制，允许优化器探索稍显尖锐的损失地形，避免过早陷入平坦区域。

Result: 证明了所提方法能够使训练过程始终保持在EoS阈值（步长与Hessian最大特征值的乘积大于2）之上；实现了非单调的损失下降；能够有效最小化模型的锐度，并显著提升了训练成功率和模型的泛化性能。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，在神经网络训练中，通过动态调整步长使其保持在“稳定性边缘”（EoS）区域，即使在非全局L-光滑的情况下，也能实现高效且稳健的训练。研究还发现，过早进入全局平坦区域可能会阻碍收敛并损害泛化能力，适当的“尖锐”训练有助于改善结果。

Abstract: The training of neural networks often entails objective functions that are not globally $L$-smooth. For these functions, it is both theoretically and practically difficult to reply to the question: what is the largest possible step size that ensures the convergence of gradient descent (GD)? We address this longstanding open question in deep learning by providing a unifying definition of "large" step sizes that requires only local Lipschitz (or even Hölder) continuity of the gradient. We design first-order adaptive methods that provably yield large step sizes and show that they operate at the edge of stability (EoS) right from the start of the training. In particular, the loss decreases nonmonotonically and the product between the step size and sharpness, i.e., the largest eigenvalue of the Hessian, stays above the EoS threshold of 2 throughout training. Using our method, we are also able to minimize the sharpness all the way down to its global minimum. Contrary to expectation, we find that encountering globally-flat regions too early in the training may both slow down convergence and jeopardize the generalization ability of the network. Exploiting a self-stabilization argument, we allow GD to enter slightly sharper valleys and turn unsuccessful training runs into very successful ones.

### [134] [Synthics: Synthetic Physics-like Datasets for Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06724)
*Jari Vepsäläinen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用贝叶斯概率上下文无关文法生成具有真实物理结构特征的合成回归数据集的方法，有效地解决了机器学习中数据获取受限的问题，且在下游任务中表现出与真实数据相当的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器学习中，获取足够的真实世界数据往往受限且成本高昂。虽然合成数据生成是解决该问题的有效途径，但关键在于合成数据必须能够忠实地反映真实观测的底层物理结构，而现有的随机方法难以保证这种结构上的严谨性和物理意义。

Method: 1. 利用贝叶斯概率上下文无关文法（BPCFG）捕捉方程库的代数结构以采样生成新方程；2. 通过非侵入式探测（non-intrusive probing）刻画方程的适用域（applicability domain）并提取变量间约束；3. 采用均匀分布与截断正态分布混合的采样策略模拟现实实验条件；4. 使用Kolmogorov-Smirnov检验对生成的合成数据进行统计验证。

Result: 1. 统计验证结果表明，本文生成的数据在八项结构特征上均与费曼方程库吻合；2. 相比之下，未经优化的纯概率文法仅能匹配其中两项特征；3. 在超参数调优任务中，基于合成数据调优的模型平均性能排名第6，显著优于随机表达式树（第10）和噪声（第19），并达到了使用真实数据调优的效果。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于贝叶斯概率上下文无关文法（BPCFG）的方法，能有效生成在代数结构上与物理方程库高度相似的合成数据集。实验证明，该方法生成的合成数据在下游任务（如超参数调优）中表现出色，能够替代真实数据，且其结构保真度远优于传统的随机表达式树方法。

Abstract: Representative data is fundamental in machine learning, as limited data hinders generalisation. Collecting sufficient real-world samples is often infeasible. Synthetic data generation offers a practical solution, but only if the generated data faithfully reflects the structure of real observations. In this paper, a method for generating synthetic regression datasets that structurally resemble physics equations from a given equation corpus is presented. The approach uses a Bayesian Probabilistic Context-Free Grammar to capture the underlying algebraic structure of the corpus, from which novel equations are sampled. To ensure the generated inputs lie within a physically meaningful domain, the applicability domain is characterised for each equation through non-intrusive probing, also recovering inter-variable constraints. Input sampling further mimics realistic experimental conditions by drawing from random sub-ranges of the valid domain with mixed uniform and truncated normal distributions. The generated data is statistically validated against the Feynman equation corpus using Kolmogorov-Smirnov tests. The generated equations match the corpus on all of the eight studied structural features, compared to only two for an unsmoothed purely probabilistic grammar, demonstrating that the Bayesian prior is essential for structural fidelity given the size of the corpus. In a downstream hyperparameter-tuning task, a gradient-boosted regressor tuned on the synthetic data picks, on average, the 6th-best configuration out of 20 on real data, matching the result of tuning on real data itself and substantially outperforming random expression trees (10th) and noise (19th).

### [136] [Learn to Match: Two-Sided Matching with Temporally Extended Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06744)
*Haijing Zong,Yancheng Liang,Boyang Zhou,Natasha Jaques*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对动态匹配市场中信息随时间演化的特征，引入了一个包含部分可观测马尔可夫博弈的框架，并推出了Learn2Match基准。研究发现，虽然强化学习（PPO）在整体福利上表现优异，但仍需结合匹配机制的结构化探索能力来降低信息摩擦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的双边匹配模型多将过程简化为针对固定偏好的即时次高斯反馈，忽略了现实中匹配信息随时间演化、面试互动及学习过程而逐步揭示的特性。因此，本文旨在填补这一空白，研究如何处理具有时间跨度的反馈信息及其对匹配决策的影响。

Method: 作者提出了一个将双边匹配建模为部分可观测马尔可夫博弈（POMG）的框架，涵盖了昂贵的预匹配筛选、有噪声的后匹配观测、演化的潜在画像以及内生的持续或解除匹配决策。并以此构建了名为“Learn2Match”的MARL基准测试平台，评估指标包括遗憾值（regret）、社会福利和信息摩擦损失。

Result: 实验发现，在具有时间扩展反馈的环境中，独立PPO算法在累积社会福利和累积遗憾值方面优于传统的强盗算法基准（CA-ETC）；然而，PPO在信息摩擦损失上较高，表明目前的端到端MARL算法尚缺乏匹配-强盗（matching-bandit）方法所具备的协调探索能力。

Conclusion: 研究表明，多智能体强化学习（MARL）在处理动态匹配市场方面展现出巨大潜力，但在应对信息摩擦和实现协调探索方面仍有提升空间。Learn2Match 为未来开发结合强化学习适应性、多臂老虎机统计严谨性以及稳定匹配机制结构性的算法提供了重要的基准平台。

Abstract: Two-sided matching markets often involve information that unfolds over time through interviews, repeated interaction, learning, and separation. Existing matching models typically reduce this process to immediate sub-Gaussian feedback about fixed preferences, missing settings where payoff-relevant information is revealed gradually and changes future matching decisions. We introduce a framework with temporally extended feedback, that formulates two-sided matching as a partially observable Markov game with costly pre-match screening, noisy post-match observations, evolving latent profiles, and endogenous continuation or dissolution. We instantiate this framework in Learn2Match, a multi-agent reinforcement-learning benchmark for dynamic matching markets. Learn2Match supports decentralized decision making over whom to interview, whom to match with, and when to dissolve a match, while evaluating policies using regret, social welfare, and an information-friction loss that measures the welfare gap caused by incomplete revelation of latent preferences. We find that independent PPO achieves higher cumulative social welfare and lower cumulative regret than the bandit-style CA-ETC baseline under temporally extended feedback, demonstrating the promise of MARL for dynamic matching markets. However, PPO still incurs higher information-friction loss, revealing that end-to-end MARL does not yet provide the coordinated exploration structure of matching-bandit methods. These results position Learn2Match as a benchmark for developing the next generation of matching-market algorithms: methods that are adaptive like RL agents, statistically disciplined like bandit algorithms, and structurally aware like stable-matching mechanisms.

### [137] [Performance Variation in Deep Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06746)
*Haruto Tanaka,A. Rupam Mahmood*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出深度强化学习算法存在严重的运行不稳定性问题，批评了现有研究对该问题评估不足的现状，并提出了一套基于百分位数的分析与可视化工具（min-max IPR 等），以更准确地刻画算法的性能鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度强化学习算法在相同配置下多次运行的结果往往存在显著性能差异（即缺乏运行鲁棒性），但现有研究多仅报告平均性能及其不确定性，这掩盖了算法性能波动的真实风险，缺乏有效的评估标准。

Method: 提出了一套基于百分位数的鲁棒性评估框架，包括用于量化性能变化的“min-max IPR”统计指标，以及用于直观展示运行间性能波动的“逐次运行百分位数高亮（run-wise percentile highlighting）”可视化方法。通过在 PPO、SAC、TD-MPC 等主流算法及 Atari 环境上的对比实验验证了该方法的有效性。

Result: 实验表明：LayerNorm 等归一化技术能有效降低 PPO 的性能波动；在多算法对比中，TD-MPC 在保证高数据效率的同时表现出最小的性能波动；而在 DQN 与 Rainbow 的对比中发现两者表现出相近的鲁棒性水平。这些发现验证了所提方法能揭示传统指标无法捕捉的性能细节。

Conclusion: 传统的均值和标准差指标难以全面刻画深度强化学习算法的运行不稳定性，而提出的基于百分位数的统计方法（如 min-max IPR）和可视化手段能够更准确、直观地量化并呈现不同运行间的性能波动，有助于研究人员更客观地评估算法的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Deep reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms often suffer from low run-to-run robustness, manifesting as significant performance variation across independent runs of identically configured agents. Although this issue poses a spectrum of challenges across research and practice, relatively few studies develop methods to evaluate it; RL research instead often reports uncertainty in the estimated mean performance. In this paper, we outline the limitations of conventional uncertainty and variation estimates, particularly their misalignment with purpose and the risk of underreporting. We then propose an alternative percentile-based statistic and visualization method, min-max IPR and run-wise percentile highlighting, respectively. These percentile-based tools are easy to interpret and rely on standard properties of sample percentiles, providing rich information about run-to-run performance variation. We demonstrate this through three case studies. First, we show that LayerNorm and penultimate-layer normalizations narrow performance variation in PPO, whereas the variation is mostly unchanged in SAC. Second, we compare PPO, SAC, TD-MPC, and TD-MPC2, and show TD-MPC exhibits the least variation while being the most data efficient among the four. Finally, in a comparison of DQN and Rainbow on five Atari environments, we show that both algorithms exhibit similar levels of performance variation.

### [138] [A Rolling-Window Framework for Churn Prediction and Behavioral Driver Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06776)

Conclusion: 研究表明，在非合同制服务环境中，精心设计的“时间框架”（Temporal Framing）比单纯的模型复杂性对实现鲁棒、可解释且易于部署的客户流失预测更为关键。该框架为动态服务环境下的流失预警提供了实用的决策支持基础。

Existing churn prediction approaches often rely on simplified temporal assumptions or single-point representations of customer behavior, which limit their ability to support continuous risk assessment, interpretability, and realistic deployment over time. This study proposes a temporally explicit churn prediction framework that models customer behavior using rolling behavioral windows, enabling repeated and instance-level churn risk estimation as customer activity evolves. Customer behavior is summarized within a fixed 30-day observation window, followed by a 30-day future churn evaluation window, ensuring a clear temporal separation between behavioral evidence and churn outcomes. The framework integrates feature-based and sequence-based learning approaches within a unified temporal design. The proposed approach is evaluated on a large-scale, real-world dataset from a non-contractual service platform. Empirical results demonstrate strong and stable predictive performance, with accuracy reaching 87.6% and ROC-AUC of 0.94 for the feature-based model, while the sequence-based model achieves recall as high as 96.1% by capturing temporal disengagement patterns. Evaluation on future unseen data confirms meaningful robustness under temporal shift, with accuracy remaining above 83% and ROC-AUC exceeding 0.91 without model retraining. Overall, the findings highlight that carefully designed temporal framing, rather than model complexity alone, is critical for achieving robust, interpretable, and deployment-ready churn prediction. The study provides a practical foundation for churn-oriented decision support in dynamic service environments.

</details>

Afterwards, we identify key constraints inherent to vehicular environments that challenge the practical deployment of M3T FedFMs, and articulate a set of forward-looking research directions to address these challenges. Furthermore, through a case study conducted on a real-world vehicular dataset (i.e., Waymo Open Dataset), we demonstrate the promise of M3T FedFMs for vehicular networks and release our implementation to facilitate reproducibility and stimulate research in this emerging area (repository: https://github.com/KasraBorazjani/vehicular-fedfm)

TL;DR: 该研究对比了联合估计与逐步估计Q矩阵对动态认知诊断模型结果的影响，发现前者在面对未知结构和项目变动时更可靠，且分析路径的选择会直接改变对学习者技能发展水平的结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在数字学习环境中，当评估项目的技能属性（Q矩阵）未知时，研究者面临“联合估计”还是“先确定结构再评估学习”的抉择。该研究旨在探讨这种决策对揭示学习者技能发展规律及后续教学报告的影响。

Method: 研究采用了动态认知诊断模型（Dynamic Cognitive Diagnostic Models）。通过将项目文本嵌入（item-text embeddings）作为未知Q矩阵的先验信息，比较了“联合估计模型”与“偏差校正后的逐步估计模型”两种分析路径，并结合仿真研究评估了两者的差异。

Result: 在针对二年级到三年级阅读游戏数据的分析中，两种方法虽均显示大部分学习者趋向掌握两项核心技能（词汇与理解），但在“三年级仍处于部分掌握状态”的学生人数估计上存在显著分歧。仿真模拟证实，联合分析在处理不确定结构和动态项目池时表现更优。

Conclusion: 在处理未知的项目-技能结构（Q矩阵）时，联合分析方法相比逐步分析方法具有更高的稳健性和可靠性，特别是在项目池随时间变化的情况下。研究结果强调，模型选择策略对理解学习者的发展路径具有实质性影响。

Abstract: Digital learning environments record learners' responses to individual items, making it possible to study the development of specific skills rather than overall scores. Drawing conclusions about learning from these data requires a model that links responses to latent skills and tracks how mastery changes over time. When the skills measured by each item are unknown, the analyst must decide whether to estimate this structure, the Q-matrix, jointly with the learning process, or to establish it first and study learning afterwards. We show that this decision can change substantive conclusions about how learners develop. Using dynamic cognitive diagnostic models, we analyse data from two reading games measuring vocabulary and comprehension from Grade 2 to Grade 3, with item-text embeddings providing prior information for the unknown Q-matrix. A joint analysis and a bias-corrected stepwise analysis agree that most learners move toward mastering both skills, but disagree about how many remain only partially proficient at Grade 3, changing how reading progress would be reported. A simulation study identifies when the two analyses diverge and shows that joint analysis is more reliable when the item-skill structure is uncertain and the item pool changes between grades. We provide R code for both analyses.

### [141] [SCALE: Scalable Cross-Attention Learning with Extrapolation for Agentic Workflow Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06820)
*Zhifei Xu,Jierui Lan,Zixuan Liang,Aiji Liang,Jinxi He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对AI代理任务调度中DRL模型难以跨集群规模泛化的问题，本文提出了SCALE框架，利用交叉注意力架构和SRR正则化技术，实现了在未见集群规模下的高效调度，且无需额外训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于深度强化学习（DRL）的代理任务调度器通常绑定于固定的集群规模，一旦服务器数量改变就需要重新训练，无法适应动态变化的异构集群环境。因此，迫切需要一种能够泛化到未见集群规模且无需微调的调度方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为SCALE（可扩展交叉注意力学习与外推）的调度器，核心包含两部分：1. 基于交叉注意力指针网络（Cross-Attention Pointer Network）的架构，使其能够通过查询机制适配任意数量的服务器；2. 引入结构化表征正则化（SRR），通过去相关损失和KL散度惩罚，稳定不同规模下特征分布的统计特性，防止分布偏移。

Result: 在16个节点的集群上训练，并直接在32和48个节点的集群上进行测试。结果显示，在48个节点规模下，相比不使用SRR的架构，SCALE将平均响应时间降低了8.9%，证实了显式正则化在缩小规模泛化差距方面的必要性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的SCALE架构通过结合交叉注意力机制和结构化表征正则化（SRR），成功解决了深度强化学习调度器在面对异构集群规模变化时的泛化难题，为大规模智能体任务调度提供了高效、可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Agentic Large Language Model (LLM) systems decompose complex tasks into workflow Directed Acyclic Graphs (DAGs) whose primitives must be scheduled on heterogeneous clusters. Existing deep reinforcement learning (DRL) schedulers are tied to a fixed cluster size and require retraining whenever the number of servers changes. We propose SCALE (Scalable Cross-Attention Learning with Extrapolation), a DRL scheduler that generalizes to unseen cluster scales without fine-tuning. SCALE employs a cross-attention pointer network where task features query against server features, so the architecture accepts any number of servers by construction. We observe, however, that permutation-invariant architecture alone does not guarantee good performance at new scales - the attention feature undergoes distribution shift as the server count grows. To counter this, we introduce Structured Representation Regularization (SRR): a decorrelation loss combined with a KL penalty toward the standard normal, which keeps feature statistics stable regardless of input size. Trained on 16 nodes and tested directly on 32 and 48 nodes, SCALE reduces average response time by 8.9% at N=48 relative to the same architecture without SRR, confirming that explicit regularization is necessary to close the scale-generalization gap.

Abstract: While deep learning has excelled in various domains, its application to sequential decision-making in finance remains challenging due to the low Signal-to-Noise Ratio (SNR) and non-stationarity of financial data. Leveraging the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), we propose \textbf{PandaAI}, a closed-loop neuro-symbolic LLM agent with market regime modeling and constrained alpha generation, which bridges general LLM reasoning with financial rigor and suppresses the financial toxicity of LLM-generated outputs. To bridge the gap between general linguistic capability and financial rigor, we fine-tune a domain-specific LLM. Furthermore, we integrate this LLM into a modular architecture and form a closed-loop system. Unlike traditional models that optimize isolated prediction metrics, \textbf{PandaAI} is designed as a neuro-symbolic agent that navigates the complex, real-world financial environment with explicit risk awareness. Extensive experiments on CSI 300 stock data show that \textbf{PandaAI} achieves a $18.2\%$ higher Rank IC and $25.7\%$ lower maximum drawdown than state-of-the-art time-series models. ### [143] [Architecture Shapes Transfer Specificity in Implicit Neural Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06827)
*D Yang Eng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究指出坐标网络中“热启动增益”并非总是源于任务结构，通过对比不同 INR 架构发现，高迁移幅度往往伴随着较低的特异性，建议引入迁移特异性评估以优化科学机器学习中的架构选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的坐标网络迁移学习通常以“热启动增益”（warm-start gain）来衡量，但这种增益究竟源于特定任务的结构信息，还是仅仅得益于通用的权重重用，目前尚不清楚。本研究旨在解构并量化这种迁移的本质来源。

Method: 研究人员跨越 SIREN、ReLU MLP 和傅里叶特征 MLP 三种隐式神经表示（INR）架构，通过控制分析测试、2D 顶盖驱动腔纳维-斯托克斯（Navier-Stokes）基准测试以及一系列 1D 偏微分方程（PDE，如热方程、粘性 Burgers 方程、非线性薛定谔方程）进行实验。采用了独立随机种子控制、同架构源控制及辅助消融实验，以区分源特定结构与通用权重重用。

Result: 实验发现：1. 迁移幅度和迁移特异性是两个独立维度；2. 傅里叶特征具有最大的结构化迁移增益，但 ReLU 架构通常表现出更高的选择性；3. 没有单一架构在所有方程中占据统治地位；4. 现有的静态诊断方法较为薄弱，且启发式缩放定律 $A_{\text{transfer}} \propto 1/Δt^2$ 在 1D 审计中被推翻。

Conclusion: 本文强调在科学机器学习中，评估迁移学习效果时不能仅看迁移幅度（transfer magnitude），必须引入“迁移特异性”（transfer specificity）作为关键诊断指标。研究表明，不同架构在结构化迁移和通用权重重用之间存在权衡，应在明确的控制条件下进行架构选择。

Abstract: Transfer in coordinate networks is often measured by warm-start gain, but whether that gain reflects source-specific structure or generic weight reuse is less clear. We study this question across three implicit neural representation (INR) families, SIREN, ReLU MLPs, and Fourier-feature MLPs, using controlled analytic tests, a 2D lid-driven-cavity Navier--Stokes benchmark, and 1D PDE reference-solution suites for heat, viscous Burgers, and focusing cubic NLS. The analytic tests use independent-seed random controls, while the PDE benchmarks use alternate same-family source controls and auxiliary ablations.
  Across settings, transfer magnitude and transfer specificity separate clearly. In a 10-seed controlled 1D geometric test, Fourier Features show the largest structured transfer ($33.1\times$), followed by SIREN ($23.0\times$) and ReLU ($10.7\times$), but ReLU is far more selective: random-control transfer is $0.41\times$ for ReLU versus $14.24\times$ for SIREN. On a controlled two-parameter 1D family, the ranking changes: ReLU gives the clearest structured-versus-control separation at default settings, whereas Fourier Features improve only after bandwidth retuning. In Navier--Stokes and the broader 1D PDE suite, no single architecture dominates every equation, yet the same pattern remains: SIREN often reuses weights broadly, whereas ReLU and, in some equations, Fourier Features are more source-selective. Static diagnostics remain weak, and the heuristic scaling law $A_{\text{transfer}} \propto 1/Δt^2$ is rejected in the implemented 1D audit.
  These results position transfer specificity as a useful diagnostic for coordinate networks and suggest that architecture selection in scientific machine learning should be evaluated under explicit control conditions, not by transfer magnitude alone.

Abstract: Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) systems operating in real-time settings must process acoustic input under strict temporal constraints, where transcription decisions are inherently made on incomplete information. This causal constraint serves as an information bottleneck on attackers, significantly limiting attack performance. Our new Semantic Gambit attack breaks this causal limitation by augmenting the adversary with predictive context derived from a Large Language Model in real-time. Our experiments show that this form of augmentation can elevate the corpus-level Word Error Rate to 35.6% -- a three-fold increase over the current state-of-the-art. Ultimately, this work reveals how common, low-latency LLM tooling can be exploited to systematically subvert real-time ASR pipelines.

### [146] [Modeling Nonlinear Feature Interactions with Product-Unit Residual Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06861)
*Ziyuan Li,Uwe Jaekel,Babette Dellen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 PURe 的新型神经网络架构，通过引入乘法单元显式建模特征间的非线性交互，在提升模型预测精度、鲁棒性及可解释性的同时，改善了模型在小样本环境下的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的 MLP 模型在处理非线性特征交互时往往表现为隐式建模，导致表示纠缠，从而损害了模型的鲁棒性和可解释性。因此，需要一种能够显式捕捉特征间交叉耦合的架构。

Method: 提出了一种产品单元残差网络（PURe），该模型将乘法产品单元（product units）与残差连接（residual connections）相结合，专门设计用于显式建模交叉特征耦合，并利用 SHAP 方法对交互模式进行了解释性分析。

Result: 实验结果表明，PURe 在合成 benchmark 和真实数据集上均表现出更优的预测性能，在处理 Gaussian 特征噪声时具有更好的鲁棒性，在小样本场景下表现出更高的效率，且通过 SHAP 分析证实其学到了更集中、结构更连贯的交互模式。

Conclusion: PURe 架构通过显式建模乘法特征交互，成功提升了神经网络在处理非线性特征关联任务时的预测准确性、鲁棒性、小样本学习能力以及模型的可解释性，优于传统的 MLP。

Abstract: Understanding nonlinear feature interactions is crucial in science and engineering, yet standard multilayer perceptrons (MLPs) often capture such interactions only implicitly, leading to entangled representations that can impair robustness and interpretability. We investigate product-unit residual networks (PURe) that integrate multiplicative product units with residual connections to explicitly model cross-feature couplings while stabilizing optimization. We conduct a systematic evaluation on an interaction-driven synthetic benchmark and two real-world datasets, assessing predictive accuracy, robustness to Gaussian feature noise, and performance under limited training data, and we compare real- and complex-valued variants under a matched parameter budget. Beyond accuracy, SHapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP)-based interaction analyses show that PURe learns more concentrated and structurally coherent interaction patterns than MLP baselines. Overall, PURe achieves competitive or improved performance, better robustness and sample efficiency in low-data regimes, and enhanced interaction-level interpretability.

</details>


### [147] [Product units in gated recurrent units improve nuclear-mass prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06866)

Abstract: The prediction of masses of atomic nuclei using machine learning can complement theoretical models and advance the exploration of poorly known domains of the nuclear chart. By integrating multiplicative interactions and product-unit transformations within recurrent units, we report significant improvements in nuclear-mass prediction. ### [148] [Evidence-Grounded Ensemble Diagnosis of 802.11 Packet Captures: A Multi-Stage Pipeline with Deterministic Reliability Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06871)
*Jerome Henry,Swadhin Pradhan,Miroslav Popovic*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对LLM分析Wi-Fi协议数据包时存在的幻觉、评估偏差及置信度失准问题，本文提出PROBE框架，通过确定性标准化、证据驱动的集成推理和模型无关的评估方法，实现了高精度、高可靠的自动化网络故障诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的802.11数据包诊断依赖专家经验，效率低下且难以扩展。尽管LLM在协议分析中展现潜力，但存在幻觉（编造事件）、置信度不准确以及在评估基准中存在严重的循环偏差问题，限制了其实际应用。

Method: PROBE采用多阶段管线处理：(1) 将PCAP数据确定性地转换为可验证的文本；(2) 结合多运行、多候选模型的集成学习与渐进式混淆技术；(3) 引入“判定感知证据框架”，将缺失证据视为判定依据；(4) 通过证据有效性、稳定性及一致性计算确定性可靠性评分，完全摒弃了不可靠的LLM自评估。此外，采用逐字段断言匹配的评估机制，消除了循环评估偏差。

Conclusion: PROBE通过证据驱动的推理框架、确定性归一化以及模型无关的评估机制，成功解决了现有LLM分析网络数据包时的幻觉、置信度失准和评估偏差问题，为网络故障诊断提供了一种可靠、可扩展且具备高准确性的自动化解决方案。

Abstract: Diagnosing 802.11 packet captures requires expert protocol knowledge, is slow, inconsistent across engineers, and unscalable. LLM-based approaches sound plausible but fabricate protocol events absent from captures (especially truncated traces), produce uncalibrated confidence scores, and suffer evaluation bias when golden references are co-produced by the model under test. We introduce PROBE (Protocol Reasoning Over evidence-Based Ensembles), a multi-stage pipeline addressing all three failures. It integrates (i) deterministic PCAP-to-text normalization with frame-level verifiability, (ii) multi-run, multi-candidate ensembles with optional cross-model second opinion and progressive obfuscation, (iii) a verdict-aware evidence framework treating absence of failure evidence as contributing evidence, and (iv) a fully deterministic composite reliability score from evidence validity, run-to-run stability, and cross-model agreement without LLM self-assessment.
  On 87 enterprise Wi-Fi captures (104 capture-reviewer pairs), single-pass LLM analysis raises weighted evidence F1 from 0.871 (expert baseline) to 0.912 but misses critical frames in 35% of cases. Naive ensemble voting drops below baseline (0.842) as majority voting amplifies conservative verdicts: 50% of confirmed failures are misclassified as 'no issue' or 'insufficient evidence.' Adding evidence-grounded reconciliation achieves 0.957 F1, a 96% auto-accept rate, and a worst-case floor above 0.70. LLM self-reported confidence clusters at 0.95 regardless of difficulty (71% report exactly 0.95), confirming it is uninformative. We also introduce a model-agnostic evaluation framework using per-field assertion matching, eliminating circular bias from model-co-produced golden references.

### [150] [Data-Constrained Language Model Pretraining: Improved Regularization and Scaling Laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06888)
*Zhiwei Xu,Shihao Wu,Hanseul Cho,Wei Hu,Yixin Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 面对预训练数据耗尽的问题，本文提出了MIR正则化方法和SoftQ扩展定律，有效提升了有限数据集下多次训练的语言模型性能及规模预测准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着预训练算力的增长速度远超高质量自然语言数据的积累速度，模型训练正逐渐进入“数据受限、算力充足”的新阶段，需通过多次遍历有限数据集（多轮训练）来优化模型性能，传统的Chinchilla等扩展定律在该场景下存在失效或误判。

Method: 1. 正则化方面：引入“掩码输入正则化”（Masked-input Regularization, MIR），即在自回归预训练基础上添加掩码序列的辅助预测损失。
2. 扩展定律方面：提出“SoftQ”扩展定律，摒弃了传统Chinchilla定律中模型规模与数据量解耦的加法形式，采用能够捕捉重复数据下交互作用的耦合建模方式。

Result: 1. MIR在72M至1.4B参数的模型上均提升了验证损失，并在1.4B参数模型上实现了下游任务性能的提升。
2. SoftQ扩展定律在数据受限实验中的拟合效果显著优于传统定律。
3. 研究量化了MIR的收益，等效于增加了约1.3倍的独有训练数据量。

Conclusion: 在数据受限的预训练环境下，结合正则化手段（如MIR）与修正后的扩展定律（SoftQ）是优化模型性能的关键。该研究证明了即使在有限数据下，通过合理的正则化和扩展建模，仍能有效提升语言模型的训练效率与最终性能。

Abstract: Classical scaling laws for language model pretraining balance model size against training dataset size under a fixed compute budget, assuming abundant data and a single pass over the corpus. As training compute grows faster than the supply of natural language data, pretraining is likely to enter a data-constrained, compute-rich regime where models train for multiple epochs over a finite dataset. We study data-constrained pretraining along two axes, regularization and scaling. For regularization, we study masked-input regularization (MIR), an auxiliary next-token prediction loss on randomly masked inputs. MIR tests whether the random masking central to diffusion language models can benefit autoregressive pretraining without architectural changes or inference overhead. Across 72M to 1.4B parameter models, we find that MIR added on top of strong weight decay improves validation loss over autoregressive strong-weight-decay-only models, with downstream gains at 1.4B. For scaling, we propose SoftQ, a scaling law that couples model size and data size to capture their interaction under repeated data. Classical alternatives such as the Chinchilla law use an additive form that decouples these terms, making them misspecified in the data-constrained regime. We find that SoftQ fits data-constrained experiments substantially better than these alternatives, and estimates MIR's gains as equivalent to roughly 1.3 times as much unique training data. We release our code at https://github.com/yixinw-lab/dc_pretrain.

</details>


### [151] [GRASP: Geometry-aware Residual Alignment for Scalable Pretraining Data Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06892)
*Yue Min,Ruining Chen,Yujun Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GRASP是一种新的交互感知数据归因框架，通过建模子集间的复杂交互，显著提升了大规模数据集筛选与评估的准确性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的可扩展数据归因方法通常假设数据效用是独立的，这种加性假设无法捕捉训练数据中存在的冗余和互补性等关键子集动态，导致归因准确性受限。

Method: 提出了GRASP框架，将归因问题重构为子集级别的反事实效用预测。该方法引入二次几何惩罚来明确建模子集间的交互作用，并结合低维特征草图（feature sketches）与严格有限下置信界选择协议，以实现大规模预训练环境下的计算效率。

Result: 实验表明，GRASP在子集重训练评估中显著优于现有可扩展基准方法，将反事实子集保真度的任务级秩相关性提升了一倍以上，并将工件构建成本降低了近一个数量级。此外，该方法在语言模型整理和跨领域视觉选择中表现出良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: GRASP通过引入交互感知模型，有效解决了传统数据归因方法无法捕捉数据间冗余与互补性的难题，为大规模预训练数据优化提供了一种高效、稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: Scalable data attribution methods typically assign isolated utility scores to individual training examples. This prevalent additive assumption fundamentally fails to capture critical subset dynamics, including data redundancy and complementary coverage. In this work, we reframe attribution as subset-level counterfactual utility prediction and introduce GRASP, an interaction-aware surrogate. Grounded in a theoretical smoothness lower bound, GRASP explicitly models subset interactions through a quadratic geometric penalty. To achieve pretraining-scale efficiency without relying on hidden oracle tuning, we couple low-dimensional feature sketches with a strictly finite lower-confidence bound selection protocol. Extensive subset-retraining evaluations demonstrate that GRASP decisively outperforms existing scalable baselines. It more than doubles the task-level rank correlation for counterfactual subset fidelity while reducing upfront artifact construction costs by nearly an order of magnitude. Downstream diagnostics further show that this scoring mechanism transfers to language model curation and cross-domain vision selection, establishing a robust foundation for optimizing massive pretraining corpora.

### [152] [TALAN: Task-Aligned Latent Adaptation Networks for Targeted Post-Training of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06902)
*Chengkai Zhang,Ziteng Liu,Junpu Wang,Zeyi Tao,Yang Wang,Sagar Chordia,Qin Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TALAN 是一种新型的潜在侧支路架构，它在微调过程中与 LoRA/DoRA 联合训练，通过引入微小的、与模型主权重正交的激活级扰动，在保持极低开销的同时，有效提升了模型在推理、数学和代码任务上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的低秩适配器（如 LoRA）虽然高效但属于任务全局参数，缺乏针对不同输入的动态调整能力；而激活干预方法虽然具备输入感知性，但通常需要额外的探测器或推理时的定向引导。研究者旨在开发一种能够结合两者优势，即在不降低模型通用能力的前提下，更有效地提升模型在推理、数学和代码任务上的性能，且无需复杂的推理时干预的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 TALAN 的架构，即“任务对齐潜在适应网络”。它作为序列条件下的潜在侧支路插入到 Transformer 的残差流中，并与低秩适配器（LoRA/DoRA）在单一监督微调（SFT）循环中联合训练。其核心机制包括：将活跃序列压缩为潜在内存，通过混合器将其转化为标记级的扰动，并利用受控的残差更新将其写回模型中。该架构可通过插入位置、内存大小等六个轴向进行灵活配置。

Result: 在 Qwen3 系列模型及四个 STEM/代码基准测试中，TALAN 均优于 LoRA 和 DoRA 基准。与 LoRA 结合使用时，平均增益为 +1.41 分；与 DoRA 结合使用时，平均增益为 +1.85 分。TALAN 仅增加了不到 1% 的可训练参数，推理开销仅为 LoRA 的 1.01-1.02 倍。内部状态分析表明，TALAN 产生了一种微小但正交的扰动，该扰动会随网络深度逐渐放大，从而产生显著的性能增益。

Conclusion: TALAN 为在标准的适配器训练框架内引入可控的激活级适应提供了一个高效且实用的平台。其通过引入正交的微小扰动，能够有效弥补现有低秩适配器（如 LoRA/DoRA）在处理复杂推理任务时的不足，实现了性能的显著提升且仅带来微小的推理开销。

Abstract: Targeted post-training aims to improve reasoning, math, and code without degrading strengths. Low-rank adapters are efficient but task-global; activation interventions are input-aware but often require separate probes, vectors, or inference-time steering. We introduce TALAN (Task-Aligned Latent Adaptation Networks), a sequence-conditioned latent side path inserted into a transformer's residual stream and co-trained with a low-rank adapter in one SFT loop. TALAN compresses the active sequence into latent memory, remixes it into token-level perturbations, and writes them back through a controlled residual update. It is configured along six axes: insertion location, memory size, mixer, writeback rule, trainability scope, and gradient scale.
  Across four Qwen3-family backbones and four STEM/code benchmarks, TALAN improves matched LoRA and DoRA baselines. With LoRA, it yields a +1.41 point cross-model mean gain, positive on all four backbones and non-negative on all 16 model-benchmark cells. With DoRA, it yields a +1.85 point mean gain, positive on all backbones and on 13 of 16 cells. Paired seed checks support positive average effects but show nontrivial variance, so we treat them as sensitivity checks. Cost is small: <1% trainable parameters relative to the backbone and 1.01-1.02x inference overhead versus matched LoRA. A Llama-3.2-1B transfer probe is also positive under LoRA and rsLoRA across seven paired seeds, supporting a transfer beyond Qwen.
  Internal-state analyses suggest TALAN is a small complementary activation intervention. The matched adapter update is 80-1,700x larger than the TALAN perturbation, yet their directions have near-zero cosine; per-layer measurements show this small orthogonal perturbation propagates and amplifies through depth. TALAN offers a practical platform for studying steerable activation-level adaptation within standard adapter-based post-training.

</details>


### [153] [The Fine-Tuning Trap: Evaluating Negative Transfer and the Role of PEFT in Sub-1B Mathematical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06920)
*Rahul Nair,Chun Tao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了超小型语言模型（<1B）的微调策略，发现针对300M以下参数的模型，全量微调会导致性能严重下滑，因此推荐使用PEFT（如LoRA/DoRA）以维持模型稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在边缘设备上部署小模型时，如何在不降低通用能力的前提下进行有效微调是一个核心挑战。研究旨在探究不同微调策略对超小模型（<1B）的影响，特别是在数学推理任务中是否存在性能退化问题。

Method: 研究人员选取了5个参数量在135M至1B之间的小型语言模型（SLMs），在数学推理任务（GSM8K、OrcaMath）上，对比了全量微调（Full FT）、LoRA和DoRA三种微调策略的性能表现，并与零样本（Zero-shot）及少样本（5-shot）上下文学习进行了基准测试。

Result: 实验发现全量微调（Full FT）会对300M以下参数的模型造成显著的性能损害（即“负迁移”）；LoRA在模式匹配任务中表现更优，而DoRA在复杂推理任务中表现更佳；在极小架构（如SmolLM2-135M）上，简单的少样本学习甚至优于全量微调。

Conclusion: 研究表明，对于参数量小于500M的超小型语言模型，应默认采用参数高效微调（PEFT）以避免性能灾难性衰退。LoRA和DoRA在不同任务上各有千秋，而全量微调（Full FT）在超小模型上极易引发负迁移。

Abstract: Deploying Small Language Models (SLMs) on edge devices requires efficient fine-tuning strategies that adapt models to new tasks without degrading their general capabilities. In this study, we benchmark five sub-1B models (135M-1B) on mathematical reasoning tasks and uncover a critical vulnerability: Full Fine-Tuning (Full FT) actively harms performance in models under 300M parameters, often dropping accuracy below zero-shot baselines. This "negative transfer" makes Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT) not just an efficiency preference, but a stability requirement. We find that while Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) and Weight-Decomposed LoRA (DoRA) perform comparably, their strengths vary by task; DoRA excels in complex reasoning (GSM8K), while LoRA dominates pattern matching (OrcaMath). In particular, Full FT is outperformed by LoRA on aligned models (Qwen2.5-0.5B) and even by simple 5-shot In-Context Learning on the smallest architectures (SmolLM2-135M). Based on these findings, we recommend defaulting to PEFT for all aligned sub-1B models and caution against Full FT for any architecture smaller than 500M parameters to prevent catastrophic forgetting. Reproduction of this work can be found at https://github.com/gulguluu/tiny-slm-finetune-compare.

</details>


### [154] [From Sampled Outcomes to Capability Distributions: Rethinking Supervision for LLM Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06924)
*Guannan Lai,Haoran Hu,Long Chen,Zhenguo Li,Han-Jia Ye*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有LLM路由方法中因单次响应带来的噪声干扰问题，本文提出了DARS框架，通过引入输入和输出端的分布特性，构建了更稳健的路由监督信号，从而提升了路由策略的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM路由方法过度依赖单一的生成结果作为能力标签，忽略了LLM生成过程的随机性，导致监督信号存在系统性噪声，进而降低了路由策略的可靠性。

Method: 提出了DARS（分布感知路由监督）框架。该框架摒弃了单一响应的监督方式，转而构建基于分布的路由监督，通过综合考虑输入端（语义等价查询）和输出端（生成随机性）的不确定性，从而获得更可靠的模型性能估计。

Result: 实验表明，基于单次响应的标签在模型选择上具有误导性；而DARS通过引入分布感知监督，构建了更稳定的性能标签，有效改善了路由模型的学习效果和最终决策行为。

Conclusion: LLM路由机制应从基于“单次响应”的观测转向基于“查询级模型能力分布”的评估。DARS证明了考虑模型行为的分布特性可以显著提升路由决策的准确性和稳定性。

Abstract: Existing LLM routing methods typically treat a model's single response to a query as its capability label for training routers. However, because LLM generation is inherently stochastic, such single-shot supervision provides only a noisy observation of a query-model pair's behavior rather than a reliable capability estimate. We show that this assumption introduces systematic noise into routing supervision, making learned routing policies less reliable. To address this issue, we propose DARS (Distribution-Aware Routing Supervision), a framework that constructs routing supervision from a distributional view of model behavior. Instead of relying on a single generated response, DARS considers uncertainty from both the input side and the output side, capturing how semantically equivalent query formulations and stochastic generations affect model performance. Based on these distribution-aware observations, DARS builds more reliable supervision signals for routing. Experiments across diverse tasks show that single-shot labels can be misleading for model selection, while distribution-aware supervision provides more stable labels and improves learned routing behavior. Our results suggest that reliable LLM routing should move beyond single-response observations and be grounded in query-level model capability distributions.

### [155] [Uniform Stability and Generalization Error of GD and SGD on Fixed-Point Parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06934)
*Jonghyun Shin,Sejun Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文分析了梯度下降（GD）和随机梯度下降（SGD）在离散参数空间（涉及舍入操作）下的泛化与稳定性，证明了离散化会显著改变算法的泛化特性，并揭示了舍入策略与算法稳定性之间复杂的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在硬件限制下，许多优化算法在离散参数空间（即进行数值舍入）上运行，但现有的优化理论大多基于实值连续空间，缺乏对离散化带来的泛化误差和稳定性影响的深入理解。

Method: 利用泛化误差、一致稳定性（uniform stability）和一致参数稳定性（uniform argument stability）分析框架，针对凸性、Lipschitz连续和光滑损失函数，分别对确定性舍入和随机舍入下的GD与SGD算法进行理论推导与下界证明。

Result: 1. 确定性舍入使GD的泛化误差从O(T/n)退化至O(T/√n)，且GD的一致稳定性变为Ω(T)，使稳定性边界失效。
2. 确定性舍入下的SGD具有非平凡的一致稳定性，其中一维情形为O(T/n)，高维情形为O(T^2/n)。
3. 随机舍入会引入与维度相关的泛化误差，这是传统实值优化中所没有的。
4. 给出了随机舍入下一致参数稳定性的紧致上界。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了离散参数空间下，舍入策略（确定性或随机性）对梯度下降算法泛化性能的根本性影响。确定性舍入会导致GD性能下降且失去稳定性保证，而SGD虽然具有鲁棒性，但其稳定性与维度高度相关。此外，随机舍入引入了维度相关的泛化误差，这与标准实值优化有本质区别。

Abstract: We analyze generalization error, uniform stability, and uniform argument stability of gradient descent (GD) and stochastic gradient descent (SGD) over discrete parameter spaces, where each update involves deterministic or stochastic rounding. We show that deterministic rounding degrades the generalization error of GD on convex, Lipschitz, and smooth loss functions, increasing the rate from $O(T/n)$ to $O(T/\sqrt{n})$, and establish matching lower bounds. We further prove that uniform stability of GD becomes $Ω(T)$, showing that stability-based generalization bounds are vacuous in this setting. In contrast, for the same losses, stochastic gradient descent with deterministic rounding admits nontrivial uniform stability guarantees, which differ qualitatively from the real-valued case and exhibit distinct dependencies on the number of iterations and the dimension: we prove tight bounds $O(T/n)$ for one dimension and $O(T^2/n)$ for higher dimensions. We also show that stochastic rounding can introduce generalization error that increases with the dimension; such a phenomenon is absent in standard real-valued optimization and in the deterministic rounding case. Finally, we provide upper bounds on uniform argument stability for stochastic rounding schemes and show that these bounds are tight when the loss can be represented as a sum of coordinate-wise functions.

### [156] [GenPO++: Generative Policy Optimization with Jacobian-free Likelihood Ratios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06967)
*Ke Hu,Shutong Ding,Panxin Tao,Jingya Wang,Ye Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GenPO++ 提出了一种利用历史状态实现高阶可逆 ODE 求解的新框架，实现了在不改变动作维度的情况下精确计算生成式策略的动作似然，消除了偏差并提高了强化学习的训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于流（Flow-based）的生成式策略在强化学习中存在局限性：要么使用有偏的似然比近似导致训练不稳定，要么通过增加伪动作（Dummy-action）来恢复精确似然，但这会扩大策略空间并增加计算开销。研究旨在寻找一种既能保持生成式策略高表现力，又能实现精确似然计算且高效的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 GenPO++ 的可逆生成式策略优化框架。该方法利用历史状态作为高阶可逆 ODE 求解器的辅助内存，实现了动作维度的精确反转，从而无需增加额外维度（伪动作）即可进行精确的似然计算，且无需计算 Jacobian 行列式。

Result: 在大型模拟控制、微调任务以及真实机器人操作任务中，GenPO++ 展现出优于或等同于现有最先进策略优化方法的性能，同时在训练稳定性和计算效率上均有显著提升。

Conclusion: GenPO++ 通过创新的可逆 ODE 求解器设计，解决了生成式策略在强化学习中似然计算的偏差与计算开销问题，为在复杂连续控制任务中应用表现力更强的生成式策略提供了高效、稳定的框架。

Abstract: Generative policies provide expressive and multimodal action distributions, making them attractive for reinforcement learning (RL) in complex continuous-control tasks. Among them, flow-based policies are especially appealing because they generate actions through deterministic transport maps. However, applying such generative policies to likelihood-based on-policy learning remains limited by the difficulty of evaluating the probability of executed actions. Existing flow RL methods either replace the true action-density ratio with approximate surrogates, which can introduce biased updates, or recover exact likelihoods through dummy-action augmentation, which enlarges the policy space and increases computation. In this work, we propose GenPO++, a reversible generative policy optimization framework that uses history states as auxiliary memory in a high-order reversible ODE solver, yielding exact inversion without changing the original action dimension. The resulting generative policy map has a log-determinant determined only by fixed solver coefficients, enabling exact and Jacobian-free likelihood-ratio computation. This design preserves the expressiveness of generative flow policies while avoiding both action ratio bias and dummy-action overhead. We evaluate GenPO++ on large-scale simulated control, fine-tuning, and real-world robotic manipulation tasks, where it achieves competitive or superior performance over state-of-the-art on-policy RL methods, while improving training stability and computational efficiency.

Two catalyst instantiations are investigated: an adaptive Multiple-Gradient Descent Algorithm-Based Catalyst (MGDA) and a predefined-weight variant that enables focused exploration when budgets are tight. Experiments on the DTLZ benchmark suite (using 2 objectives and 10 decision variables) show that predictive gradient catalysis can deliver significant acceleration compared to other acquisition functions (EHVI, AugTch, tMPoI, SAF) when surrogates are accurate, particularly for stationary problems.

### [160] [RASFT: Rollout-Adaptive Supervised Fine-Tuning for Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07006)
*Yongliang Miao,Fengyuan Liu,Wei Shi,Yanguang Liu,Fei Sun,Na Zou,Mengnan Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对传统 SFT 强迫模型模仿单一路径导致过拟合的问题，RASFT 提出了一种根据模型当前推理能力动态调整专家监督力度的训练框架，显著提升了模型在数学和代码推理任务上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的有监督微调（SFT）通过强迫模型模仿单一专家路径进行训练，容易导致模型过拟合于特定的表面形式，并抑制了模型自身发现更优推理路径的能力。

Method: 提出了“Rollout-Adaptive Supervised Fine-Tuning (RASFT)”框架，该方法通过验证策略生成的路径来评估问题解决难度，动态调整专家监督：在模型能力不足时强化专家引导；在模型已具备可靠能力时，减少对特定路径的模仿并利用正确的自主生成轨迹。此外，引入了基于冻结参考模型的截断逆比率约束，以防止策略过度偏移。

Result: 在六个数学推理基准和两个代码推理基准上的实验表明，RASFT 在性能上优于标准的 SFT、其他 SFT 变体以及典型的强化学习方法。

Conclusion: RASFT 框架通过动态调整专家监督强度并引入策略漂移约束，证明了在推理任务中，相比于传统的刚性模仿学习，根据模型当前能力水平进行自适应学习能更有效地提升大模型的逻辑推理性能。

Abstract: Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) is a prevailing method for adapting large language models to reasoning tasks by imitating offline expert demonstrations, often treating a single expert trajectory as the target behavior. However, reasoning is not simple path imitation: rigidly following one demonstrated solution may overfit to surface forms and suppress the model's own reasoning distribution. We propose Rollout-Adaptive Supervised Fine-Tuning (RASFT), a policy-aware SFT framework that calibrates expert supervision according to problem-level solvability estimated from verified on-policy rollouts. For each problem, RASFT strengthens expert guidance when the current policy struggles, while relaxing rigid imitation and incorporating correct self-generated trajectories when the model already exhibits reliable reasoning behavior. To preserve useful reasoning priors, RASFT further introduces a clipped inverse ratio between the frozen reference model and the current policy to constrain excessive policy drift. Experiments across multiple models on six mathematical reasoning benchmarks and two code reasoning benchmarks show that RASFT achieves better overall performance than SFT, SFT variants, and representative RL methods. The code is available at https://github.com/zjd1sq/RASFT.

</details>


### [161] [A Geometric View for Understanding Concept Learning and Neuron Interpretation in Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07007)
*Chenhao Zhang,Chris Lin,Su-In Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文为稀疏自编码器（SAE）中的概念学习提供了一个统一的几何框架，通过集合对齐理论将概念学习形式化，并利用概念格分析神经元与概念之间的复杂映射，从而解释了SAE中常见的特征分裂与层级现象，为理解神经元解释性提供了理论基石。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管稀疏自编码器（SAE）在提升神经网络可解释性方面表现出色，但目前对于“概念”及“概念学习”缺乏严谨的数学定义。为了深入理解SAE如何学习特征以及为何会出现特征分裂等现象，作者旨在建立一个统一的几何与集合论框架，以实现对神经元解释的科学量化。

Method: 本文将“概念”形式化为数据集的子集，并将“概念学习”建模为人类定义概念与模型诱导概念之间的集合对齐问题。通过引入检测（detection）、分离（separation）和近似（approximation）三种学习强度，研究导出了神经元能够表征概念的几何条件、误差界限及容量约束，并结合形式概念分析（Formal Concept Analysis）通过概念格揭示了神经元与概念之间的多对多关系。

Result: 研究表明，概念的可解释性受限于其几何特性及SAE的稀疏性和容量。实验证实了该框架能有效解释SAE中的特征分裂、吸收及层级关系等现象，并揭示了不同参数设置（如SAE大小、稀疏度）对概念学习效果的定量影响。此外，研究发现模型诱导的特征与人类直觉概念之间往往存在复杂的非对齐结构。

Conclusion: 本研究构建了一个统一的几何框架来理解稀疏自编码器（SAE）中的概念学习与神经元解释。通过集合论的视角，该框架不仅揭示了SAE在处理特征分裂、吸收和层次结构时的内在机制，还明确了概念学习的理论极限与约束，为评估和优化SAE的解构能力提供了坚实的数学基础。

Abstract: We propose a unified mathematical framework for a geometric understanding of concept learning and neuron interpretation in sparse autoencoders (SAEs). While SAEs improve interpretability of neural networks by learning sparse feature representations, a principled definition of ''concept'' and ''learning'' remains unclear. We formalize concepts as sets of data points and cast concept learning as a set-alignment problem between human-defined and model-induced concepts. This formulation distinguishes three increasingly strong notions of learning -- detection, separation, and approximation -- and yields geometric conditions, error bounds, and capacity constraints for when concepts can be represented by individual neurons or multi-neuron units. It also provides a set-theoretic account for common SAE phenomena, including feature splitting, feature absorption, feature families, and hierarchical concepts. Finally, we connect concept learning and neuron interpretation through formal concept analysis, showing that the two directions need not agree and that their many-to-many structure can be organized by concept lattices. Experiments on synthetic data with ReLU and Top-$K$ SAEs illustrate the theory and reveal the effects of SAE size and sparsity on concept learning.

</details>


### [162] [CF-JEPA: Mask-free forward prediction with asymmetric encoder utilization for time-series representation learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07031)
*Jaehoon Lee,Sunghyun Sim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CF-JEPA 是一种创新的无掩码时序自监督学习框架，通过多时间跨度向前预测取代掩码机制，并巧妙利用在线与目标编码器的特征不对称性，在分类、预测和异常检测任务中显著提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的时序自监督学习（如对比学习和掩码建模）存在缺陷：对比学习受限于正负样本构建难题；而基于掩码的方法则破坏了时序信号的连续性。现有 JEPA 变体同样依赖掩码，未能彻底解决时序信号的断裂问题。因此，作者旨在开发一种无掩码、能保持时序连续性并充分利用时序内在规律的新型自监督学习架构。

Method: 提出了一种名为 CF-JEPA 的无掩码架构。该方法不再依赖掩码，而是采用多时间跨度向前预测策略：以随机裁剪作为上下文视图，并在时间轴向前预测短、中、长期未来表征。同时，通过分析单次训练中在线编码器（高秩、判别性强）与 EMA 目标编码器（低秩、平滑性好）的不对称性，为不同任务匹配最适宜的编码器。
