<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网络重构方法大多依赖于特定的扩散模型假设，当实际扩散机制与假设不符时，这些方法的性能会显著下降。因此，作者旨在开发一种无需预先指定扩散机制、能够从级联数据中稳健且准确地恢复隐藏影响网络的通用方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为CascadeNet的机器学习框架。核心思路是利用单步转换函数的雅可比矩阵（Jacobian）来表征潜在影响结构。该方法首先构建一个灵活的转换函数估计器，随后引入基于Riesz表示子的Neyman正交去偏技术，以确保所估计的雅可比矩阵具有$\sqrt{n}$-一致性和渐近正态性，从而实现对网络结构的有效统计推断。

Result: 在模拟实验中，CascadeNet在九种常见的扩散数据生成过程中均表现出最高的网络恢复准确性；在新冠疫情传播的实证应用中，CascadeNet重构的传播网络与真实人口流动数据呈现高度显著的相关性，显著优于基准方法。

Conclusion: CascadeNet通过利用雅可比矩阵的无模型特性，成功解决了网络重构中因模型假设偏差导致的性能下降问题，为从动态级联数据中推断潜在影响网络提供了一种稳健且具备统计可解释性的通用框架。

Abstract: Many important outcomes unfold as dynamic cascades, including product adoption, disease spread, financial distress, and information diffusion. A central challenge is to recover the hidden influence network behind these cascades. Existing methods typically assume a specific diffusion model, and their performance degrades substantially when that assumption is misspecified. We propose CascadeNet, a Jacobian-based machine learning framework for network recovery that does not require specifying a diffusion mechanism. The key idea is that the underlying influence structure can be characterized by the Jacobian of the one-step transition function. CascadeNet first constructs a flexible estimator of the transition function, and further applies Neyman-orthogonal debiasing via the Riesz representer, so that the debiased Jacobian is $\sqrt{n}$-consistent and asymptotically normal, enabling formal inference on the network structure. We validate CascadeNet in both a simulation exercise and a real-world empirical application. In simulations, where the data-generating process is known, CascadeNet achieves the highest network recovery accuracy across nine common data-generating processes. In an empirical application to COVID-19 transmission across Spain's 52 provinces, CascadeNet recovers transmission networks that are significantly correlated with the true inter-province mobility network, whereas networks recovered by baseline methods show no significant alignment with the ground truth.

</details>


### [208] [CoMetaPNS: Continually Meta-learning Personalized Neural Surrogates for Cardiac Electrophysiology Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07488)
*Ryan Missel,Xiajun Jiang,Linwei Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种持续元学习框架，通过引入持续贝叶斯高斯混合模型，使个性化心脏神经代理模型能够在线处理序列数据并自主识别任务来源，有效解决了计算成本高及灾难性遗忘的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对个性化心脏模拟的神经代理模型在面对临床场景中持续到来的数据流时，通常需要全量重训练以避免灾难性遗忘，这导致计算成本过高且在实际应用中难以实施。此外，现有模型往往难以在没有预设任务标识的情况下识别数据来源。

Method: 提出了一种结合持续贝叶斯高斯混合模型（CBGMM）与内存缓冲区的持续元学习框架。该方法通过CBGMM识别输入数据的动态源（已知或未知），并利用元学习实现对个性化神经代理的高效更新，从而在处理序列数据时避免了灾难性遗忘。

Result: 在合成心脏数据上的实验结果表明，该框架在模拟预测性能、计算可扩展性以及对抗灾难性遗忘的能力方面，均显著优于现有的基准方法。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的持续元学习框架有效解决了心脏个性化模拟中数据序列化到来时面临的灾难性遗忘问题，实现了无需全量重训练的高效模型更新，为临床环境下的动态模型部署提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Personalized virtual heart simulations face challenges in model personalization and computational cost. While neural surrogates offer state-of-the-art solutions, they typically address either efficient personalization or training generalizable models. Recent work reframes this by learning the process of personalizing a surrogate using limited subject-specific context data, through few-shot generative modeling with set-conditioned surrogates and meta-learned amortized inference. These methods, however, assume a static and diverse training distribution with known task identifiers. When new data becomes available, they require costly retraining with all prior data to avoid catastrophic forgetting - a phenomena where the model forgets earlier tasks when trained on new ones. This is a major limitation in clinical settings where often unlabeled data arrives sequentially and full retraining is infeasible. This paper presents a new continual meta-learning framework to achieve personalized neural surrogates able to not only continually integrate information but also identify whether incoming data stems from a known or unknown dynamics source. By leveraging a continual Bayesian Gaussian Mixture Model over a memory buffer, our framework can infer the identifiers and relationships of data over time - required for effective meta-learning. Empirical results on synthetic cardiac data demonstrate superior simulation forecasting, computational scalability, and resilience to catastrophic forgetting compared to existing baselines.

### [209] [Second-Order Path Kernel Interpolation Formulas in Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07495)
*Jin Guo,Roy Y. He,Jean-Michel Morel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过引入曲率加权项和随机噪声耦合项，将神经网络预测的一阶路径核理论扩展至二阶，更精确地刻画了随机梯度下降及其动量变体下的模型训练动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络的预测行为与训练数据之间的关系是深度学习理论的核心。尽管一阶路径核公式已能描述确定性梯度下降的预测，但对于更复杂的优化设置（如随机梯度下降、动量优化）及模型的高阶几何特性，现有的一阶描述不够精确。本文旨在完善这一理论，提供能涵盖二阶效应的更通用的插值公式。

Method: 本文在Pedro Domingos提出的基于优化路径的一阶插值公式基础上，利用泰勒展开和随机微积分技术推导了二阶项。具体方法包括：引入曲率加权插值项来捕捉模型的二阶几何特性；通过分析小批量梯度噪声的协方差，推导了随机优化中的采样诱导分量；并利用动量项的数学处理扩展了动量SGD的表示，最后通过浓度不等式对终端预测的波动范围进行了估计。

Result: 1. 建立了神经网络预测的二阶插值公式，包含曲率加权项；2. 针对随机梯度下降（SGD），明确了由小批量梯度噪声协方差诱导的特定成分；3. 将该框架成功扩展至动量SGD，证明了其插值结构保持不变，仅权重受内存相关因子影响；4. 导出了终端预测的浓度估计，量化了预测结果围绕二阶表示的波动范围。

Conclusion: 该研究通过推导出二阶插值公式，扩展了关于神经网络预测与训练数据之间关系的理论框架。研究结果不仅揭示了曲率和随机梯度噪声在预测中的作用，还证明了这种插值结构在动量SGD中的鲁棒性，为理解神经网络的训练行为提供了更精确的数学描述。

Abstract: Understanding how training data shape neural network predictions is a central problem in modern learning theory. In 2020, Pedro Domingos proposed an interpolation formula valid for every model learned by deterministic gradient descent. It expresses the model's prediction as an integral, along the optimization path, of a data-dependent kernel that aligns the model's gradients at the test and training data. Such a first-order characterization remains valid for models trained with batch-based stochastic optimization. In this paper, we develop second-order forms of these interpolation formulas. We show that the leading path-kernel interpolation is supplemented by a curvature-weighted interpolation term. For stochastic gradient descent, an additional sampling-induced component appears, coupling the curvature of the prediction with the covariance of mini-batch gradient noise. We also extend the representation to stochastic gradient descent with momentum, where the interpolation structure is preserved but with the weights modified by a memory-related factor. Moreover, we establish a concentration estimate for the terminal prediction, identifying the fluctuation scale around the expected second-order representation. Together, these results provide a refinement of the path-kernel interpretation of neural network prediction.

</details>


### [210] [Accelerated Decentralized Stochastic Gradient Descent for Strongly Convex Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07496)
*Ming Sun,Kun Yuan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型去中心化随机优化算法 MG-ADSGD，首次实现了在强凸问题中同时获得关于条件数和网络拓扑的加速收敛与高效通信，提供了当前学术界最优的通信复杂度理论界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在去中心化随机优化中，现有的确定性方法已能实现对条件数 $\kappa$ 和网络谱间隙 $1-\beta$ 的双重加速，但在随机优化领域，尚无现有算法能同时实现这两方面的优化性能。研究旨在弥补这一技术差距，提升大规模网络学习中的通信效率。

Method: 提出了一种名为“多轮加速去中心化随机梯度下降（MG-ADSGD）”的算法。该方法结合了 Nesterov 型原始-对偶外推技术（用于加速优化）与多轮快速 gossip 平均（用于提升共识精度），通过将 gossip 通信深度与小批量（mini-batch）采样规模进行耦合，在降低梯度方差的同时提升了通信效率。

Result: 理论分析表明，MG-ADSGD 的通信复杂度达到了 $\widetilde{\mathcal O}\left( \frac{\sigma^2}{\mu n\epsilon}\log\frac{1}{\epsilon} + \sqrt{\frac{\kappa}{1-\beta}}\log\frac{1}{\epsilon} \right)$。这一结果在去中心化强凸随机优化领域达到了最优的通信复杂度，且对 $\epsilon$ 的对数项不依赖。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 MG-ADSGD 算法通过巧妙地耦合通信轮数与小批量大小，成功解决了去中心化随机优化中难以同时获得加速收敛率（关于条件数 $\kappa$）和高效通信（关于网络谱间隙 $1-\beta$）的挑战，实现了目前已知最优的通信复杂度理论界。

Abstract: Decentralized stochastic optimization is a fundamental paradigm for large-scale learning over networks, where agents communicate only with their neighbors and no central coordinator is required. For strongly convex problems, communication efficiency is mainly determined by the condition number \(κ=L/μ\) and the network spectral gap \(1-β\). Although deterministic decentralized methods can simultaneously achieve accelerated \(\sqrtκ\) and \(1/\sqrt{1-β}\) dependences, no existing stochastic method attains both improvements at once. In this paper, we propose \emph{Multi-Gossip Accelerated DSGD} (MG-ADSGD), a decentralized stochastic algorithm that combines Nesterov-type primal--dual extrapolation with multi-round fast gossip averaging. The key idea is to couple the gossip depth with the mini-batch size so that additional communication rounds simultaneously improve consensus accuracy and reduce gradient variance. We show that MG-ADSGD achieves the communication complexity \[ \widetilde{\mathcal O}\!\left( \frac{σ^2}{μnε}\log\frac{1}ε +
\sqrt{\fracκ{1-β}}\log\frac{1}ε \right), \] where \(ε\) denotes the target accuracy, \(n\) is the number of nodes, and \(σ^2\) is the gradient variance. To the best of our knowledge, this bound yields the best currently available communication complexity for decentralized stochastic strongly convex optimization, up to logarithmic factors that are independent of $ε$.

</details>
